Six Apprentices Poisoned by Eating Yellow Croaker and Celery; All Recover After Injections and Medication 134

At the Xiong Yuanchang foundry at No. 8 Changqing Lane, Dong Yalu Road, Hongkou, yesterday morning around 7:00 AM, the workers gathered for breakfast. Six of the apprentices ate leftover yellow croaker and celery, but around 2:00 PM in the afternoon, they all complained of abdominal pain and looked pale. The manager of the foundry used a car to send them to Tongren Hospital, where doctors diagnosed them with poisoning. They were given medication and injections and recovered. They were discharged from the hospital around 6:00 PM. The names are listed below: Lu Youkang, 17 years old, from Haimen; Wang Cirong, 26 years old, from Wuxi; Xiong Liangzhi, 17 years old, from Hubei; Xiong Yuanjin, 22 years old, from Hubei; Pan Asi, 16 years old, from Wuxi; Zhao Houzhi, 21 years old.

French Concession: Xieshunxiang Robbed Again; Three of the Thieves Were the Same Ones from the Previous Two Times 135

Ling Junxiang, from Ningbo, has been operating the Xieshunxiang cotton cloth store at No. 115-117, a double-fronted storefront opposite Baoyu Lane on Ningxing Street (i.e., Shicai Street) in the French Concession for many years. He is skilled in business and a leader in the cotton cloth industry. In the past, his business was thriving, but in recent years, due to the sluggish business climate, retail and wholesale transactions have declined daily, barely covering expenses. Because of his past fame, he has been coveted by bandits. At the end of the Lunar New Year last year and on February 6th of this year, he was robbed twice, with losses ranging from 200 to 300 yuan each time. Ling reported the incidents to the police and requested an investigation, but the case has not been solved. Unexpectedly, yesterday (the 28th) at 6:30 PM, another seven bandits came, all dressed in silk long jackets and felt hats, well-dressed and unlike bandits. Two people were outside acting as lookouts, and five bandits entered the store, speaking in a northern accent. Because the store had been robbed twice, the accounting room was surrounded by wooden boards and iron doors, leaving only a hole to pass silver coins. The iron door was also equipped with a secret lock, making it difficult for outsiders to enter. Moreover, the silver coins collected from the store were sent to the bank after reaching 100 yuan. Therefore, when the five bandits arrived at the accounting room, they could not find a way in. While they were hesitating, Ling Tinghua, the owner's nephew, saw them inside and recognized three of the bandits as the same ones who had robbed the store in the previous two times. He ran upstairs and blew the whistle. The bandits, hearing the alarm, knew that they could not stay long and rushed out of the store, fleeing westward into Baoyu Lane. Afterwards, the store reported the incident to the Dazimingzhong police station, and the head of the station sent detectives to investigate and await further investigation.

Replacing the Pond Water of the Yu Garden's Zigzag Bridge 136

The water in the pond under the Zigzag Bridge in the Yu Garden in this city is unclean, which is detrimental to public health and the survival of the fish. The Chinese Animal Protection Association, in conjunction with the Municipal Public Security Bureau, has taken measures to pump out the dirty water in the pond. The association has also consulted with the Shanghai Inland Tap Water Company to fill the pond with clean water for three hours every night, for three consecutive nights, which can fill the pond. The association has also hired workers to catch the turtles and fish in the pond that eat small fish and send them to the large pond in Dachang to release them. From now on, the fish in the pond under the Zigzag Bridge can swim freely in clean water.

Page 10

Three Crew Members of the Lian'an Ship Transferred to Court for Investigation; Ministry Revokes Their Certificates 137

Regarding the case of the Sanbei Company's Wanxiang ship colliding with the Lian'an passenger ship near the Xiaogushan lighthouse in the upper reaches of the Yangtze River in December of the year before last, resulting in the sinking of the Lian'an and the drowning of more than 200 people, the arbitration result has punished the responsible crew members and notified the shipping companies in Shanghai. The details are as follows:

Investigation Result: Because more than 200 people drowned in this case, an arbitration committee was organized in Hankou. The Ministry of Transportation and the Navy each sent special commissioners to investigate and impartial persons to conduct on-site investigations. The result was that the Lian'an ship's red and green lights alternately appeared, making it impossible for the Wanxiang ship to avoid it. Therefore, the responsibility and compensation for the deaths and injuries should be borne by the party that caused the accident. The report and judgment were written by Shen Jiyun, the general shipowner of the China Merchants Steam Navigation Company, and announced in Hankou. If the Lian'an side was dissatisfied, they could file an appeal within the legal deadline. The Sanbei Wanxiang ship bears no responsibility.

Transferred to Court: Because the drowned were armed soldiers, the Hankou Maritime Bureau and the arbitration committee reported this case to the Military Affairs Commission for review. Now, Military Affairs Commission Order No. 182 instructs that the Lian'an ship, which caused the accident, has sunk into the river. The responsible crew members of the ship, the first mate Zhang Shaobo, the second mate Wang Dongyin, and the river pilot Xiao Yanqing, were responsible for negligence in performing their duties, resulting in the sinking of the ship and the drowning of more than 200 people. The Military Affairs Commission has ordered that Zhang, Wang, and Xiao be transferred to the court for investigation according to law.

Certificates Revoked: The Military Affairs Commission sent a letter to the Ministry of Transportation, instructing it to order all shipping companies across the country to revoke the certificates of the first mate Zhang Shaobo, the second mate Wang Dongyin, and the river pilot Xiao Yanqing, if they have obtained certificates. In the future, if they apply for crew positions at shipping companies, they should not be hired. The Ministry has notified the Shanghai Maritime Bureau and the state-owned and private shipping companies in Shanghai of this order, instructing them to comply with it.

Shanghai Bank Held Shareholders' Meeting Yesterday 138

Trust Department Established, Entrusted to the Board of Directors for Handling. Supervisors Lin Kanghou and Two Others Re-elected.

Shanghai Commercial & Savings Bank held its 20th Annual General Meeting of Shareholders at the Ningbo Road headquarters meeting hall yesterday afternoon at 2 p.m. It was resolved to establish a trust department and re-elect three supervisors. The details are recorded below:

Shareholders' General Meeting: Shareholders representing 29,819 shares, accounting for 15,408 votes, attended, exceeding the legal quorum. Chairman Zhuang Dezhi reported the purpose of the meeting, followed by General Manager Chen Guangfu reporting on the business situation for the year 1934, and Supervisor Lin Kanghou reporting on the audit situation. Regarding the proposed application for establishing a trust department, it was resolved to entrust it to the board of directors for handling. The supervisors were re-elected, with Lin Kanghou, Xue Minlao, and Luo Yuesheng receiving the most votes and being re-elected. The meeting adjourned at 3:30 p.m.

Business Report: The bank's business report for 1934 stated: "In its operations, the bank has consistently adhered to its established prudent policies in order to adapt to the environment. It does not seek luck or excessive profits, but strives for the safety of loans and investments. At the same time, in order to serve society, it contributes its assistance to the improvement of the national economy within the scope of its capabilities. Over the past year, all types of business have fortunately made progress, as reported separately below: Deposits and Loans: (A) Deposits: At the end of 1934, the total deposits of the entire bank, including commercial and savings deposits, amounted to $158,159,145.36. Compared with 1933, the amount increased by $14,608,754.98. Current deposits increased by $2,735,315.00, fixed deposits increased by $6,736,875.39, and savings deposits increased by $5,136,564.59. (B) Loans: In 1934, the total amount of loans from the entire bank was $156,504,389.98, an increase of $25,165,828.05 compared with the end of 1933. Status of Public Reserve and Business Preparation: In order to further enhance the security of deposits and to prepare for future increases in deposits, the bank, with the approval of the board of directors at the end of 1933, increased the public reserve fund to $4 million. This was reported at the previous shareholders' meeting. In May of this year, the board of directors' regular meeting further resolved to increase it to $5 million. At the end of the year, another $100,000 was withdrawn from the surplus item as a public reserve fund, totaling $5.1 million, which has exceeded the bank's capital of $100,000. At the same time, the business reserve fund has also been continuously increased to $2.25 million, which can be said to be a generous protection for the interests of depositors. Business Status of the Savings Department: At the end of 1934, the total savings deposits of the entire bank were $38,439,419.12, an increase of $5,136,564.59 compared with the end of 1933. Among them, current savings increased by $2,601,100.08, and fixed savings increased by $1,535,464.51. Loans at the end of 1934, including those placed in the commercial department, were $34,689,964.62, an increase of $3,167,212.42 compared with the end of 1933. In terms of type, one is secured loans. At the end of 1934, they amounted to $19,988,935.26, an increase of $11,108,317.72 compared with the previous year, accounting for more than half of the total loans. Among them, securities collateral loans accounted for 35%, agricultural product and rural cooperative loans accounted for 32%, real estate collateral loans accounted for 27%, and deposit certificate and passbook collateral loans accounted for 6%. One is securities purchase. At the end of 1934, it was $7,796,199.53, an increase of $3,077,320.87 compared with the end of 1933, an increase of about 67%. The reason for the increase is that the Savings Bank Law stipulates that savings banks must have one-quarter of the total savings deposits in government bonds, treasury bills, and other assets deposited in the Central Bank as a guarantee for deposits. In order to meet this need, securities purchases have shown a sharp increase. One is deposits in the commercial department. At the end of 1934, it was $6,904,829.83, a decrease of $11,018,426.17 compared with the end of 1933, a decrease of about 64%. This is because the Savings Bank Law imposes restrictions on deposits in the commercial department. In short, the use of savings funds has generally complied with the provisions of the Savings Bank Law. General Situation of Foreign Exchange Department: The volatility of the foreign exchange market this year is as intense as in the past. Coupled with the shrinking of foreign trade, foreign exchange operations are fraught with difficulties. The department's business has always been very stable, and it continues not to seek luck or engage in speculation. Therefore, even under difficult circumstances, it still has considerable progress. In terms of import and export documentary bills, export documentary bills have increased slightly compared with the previous year, and import documentary bills have decreased by about 12%. However, collections of import bills have doubled. The total amount of the two is still greater than in the previous year. Remittances and purchases of bills are similar to those in the previous year. This is because the foreign exchange released this year is longer, and the value is reduced when calculated in our national currency. If expressed in foreign currency, it is also greater than in the previous year. However, customs duty trading has decreased by 40% compared with the previous year. Sales of traveler's checks and traveler's letters of credit have increased by almost one letter compared with the previous year. In addition, in terms of foreign currency deposits, the total amount at the end of this year has increased by about one-third compared with the end of last year, with current deposits increasing the most. In short, all kinds of business in the department are in a steady process of progress. The business reserve fund, in addition to writing off a small number of bad debts, is also increasing year by year, and its foundation can be called strong. General Situation of the Agricultural Department: In order to serve the rural community and promote agricultural cooperation, an agricultural cooperative loan department was established in 1933, and branches were established in the Nanjing, Zhengzhou, and Changsha sub-branches to handle loans for marketing cooperation, credit cooperation, and agricultural warehouses. The total amount of loans was more than 1.02 million yuan, which greatly benefited farmers. It is also quite secure for the bank. This year, it continued to proceed, and the agricultural cooperative loan department was changed to the agricultural department. Agricultural sections were established in Nanjing, Bengbu, Jinan, Xi'an, Changsha, Hankou, Guangzhou, and other sub-branches. The business area covered Jiangsu, Zhejiang, Anhui, Shandong, Henan, Shaanxi, Shanxi, Hubei, Hunan, and nine provinces. The total amount of loans was more than 4.44 million yuan, an increase of more than four times compared with the previous year, which is a major progress. Among them, 90% are marketing cooperation loans and agricultural warehouse loans, and credit cooperation loans only account for about 8%. The bank believes that a commercial bank engaged in agricultural lending can only be limited to the turnover of short-term funds, and for the sake of prudent operation, it is especially important to emphasize the credit of goods. Therefore, most of the loans are short-term and mostly secured by commodities. Judging from the distribution trend of various agricultural loans this year, it is sufficient to prove that it can still follow this purpose and proceed. Since 1933, the accounting of the agricultural department has been independent of the commercial department. This year, because it is still in the trial stage, the cost of surveying new areas is also huge, so the expenditure is large, and the income and expenditure can only be balanced. However, all loans released can be returned on time, reducing bad debts and other matters, which can be gratifying.

Distribution of Net Profit: The net profit for 1934 was $936,061.33, an increase of $99,058.96 compared with 1933. The general distribution is listed as follows: (1) The net profit for the first half of the year was $412,264.92, plus the accumulated balance of $14,956.68 from the previous period, totaling $427,221.60. It was resolved by the board of directors on July 25 to distribute as follows: (1) Pay each shareholder a public interest of 2.5% and a bonus of 2.5% for the first half of the year, totaling $250,000. (1) Pre-withdraw staff remuneration of $100,000, and the remaining balance of $77,221.60 will be transferred to the next period's account. (1) The net profit for the second half of the year was $523,796.41, plus the accumulated balance of $77,221.60 from the previous period, totaling $601,018.01. It was resolved by the board of directors on January 21, 1935, to distribute as follows: (1) Deposit $100,000 as a public reserve fund. (1) Pay each shareholder a public interest of 2.5% and a bonus of 2.5% for the second half of the year, totaling $250,000. (1) Remuneration for directors and supervisors is $10,000. (1) Remuneration for general and deputy managers and bonuses for staff is $210,000, and the remaining balance of $31,018.01 will be transferred to the next period's account.

American Military Vehicle Ran Over and Killed a Rickshaw Puller. The Family Demands Compensation. Requests the Forwarding of a Letter to the US Consul in Shanghai 139

The Xin Xin News Agency reported that Yu Ji Shi, the mother of Yu Wei Wang, the rickshaw puller who was run over and killed by a military vehicle of the US Navy Fourth Regiment in the French Concession, has submitted a petition to Mayor Wu and others due to her son's tragic death and impoverished state, as well as the lack of means for the surviving orphans and widows. She requested that a letter be forwarded to the US Consul in Shanghai, requesting compensation. Her original petition stated: "Presenting this petition because my only son was tragically run over and killed by an American military vehicle, and I am old and helpless. Requesting permission for relief and promptly forwarding a letter requesting compensation. The petitioner is currently 72 years old and has one son named Yu Wei Wang, who is 28 years old this year. He has been pulling rickshaws for a living at Su Li's house at No. 20 Baoan Road in the Nanshi area of this port. The entire family of five, old and young, has relied on Yu Wei Wang's livelihood for many years. On March 16th of this year at about 5 p.m., the deceased Yu Wei Wang was pulling a rickshaw with the registration number 10821 of the French Concession, traveling from east to west on the left side of the road at the intersection of Wang Zhi Road and Beile Road in the French Concession. Suddenly, a military vehicle of the US Navy Fourth Regiment stationed in China came speeding from behind the deceased without honking its horn, causing the deceased to be unable to avoid it. In addition to the rickshaw with the registration number 10821 being completely destroyed, the deceased was killed on the spot due to being run over. The situation was extremely tragic. At that time, the military vehicle was taken to the French Concession Police Station, and the investigation showed that the American soldier should be fully responsible. However, due to extraterritoriality, the French Concession was unable to handle it according to law and transferred the military vehicle to the commander of the Navy Fourth Regiment, who sent someone to take it away. The outcome is still unknown. I think that my son Yu Wei Wang died tragically, which is extremely pitiful, and his death was also extremely desolate. The petitioner and the orphans and widows have a long way to go in the future, and what will they rely on for their livelihood? I want to seek legal relief, but due to the jurisdiction of consular trials, it is difficult to proceed. As a last resort, I specially submit the whole story and implore your (government) (bureau) (association) to grant relief and allow me to forward a letter to the US Consulate General in Shanghai to promptly provide compensation, so that the spirit of the deceased can be comforted, and the lives of the orphans and widows can be maintained, so as to emphasize humanity. This would be a great favor." Respectfully presented to Wu, Mayor of the Shanghai Municipal Government; Wu, Director of the Shanghai Municipal Government Social Affairs Bureau; the Shanghai Citizens' Federation of the Second Special District; and the Shanghai French Concession Taxpaying Chinese Association.

Da Hu Bank Held Shareholders' Meeting Yesterday. Jin Runxiang and Others Elected as Supervisors 141

This city's Da Hu Bank held its third annual general meeting of shareholders in the conference room on the second floor of the bank yesterday, reporting on business and re-electing supervisors. The details are recorded separately below:

Meeting Situation: Shareholders Zhu Meixian, Luo Qinghua, Zheng Xiaozhou, Shen Jinfu, Zheng Zenan, Lang Zhihao, Li Zuqing, Yu Guozhen, Wang Hong, Ma Shaoquan, Bian Chongxian, Lin Qiong'an, and others, totaling 78 people, attended, representing 2542 shares. Yu Guozhen chaired the meeting. After performing the etiquette, the business situation was first reported, followed by Supervisor Li Heqing reporting on the accounts. Then, the supervisors whose terms had expired were re-elected. Li Heqing, Jin Runxiang, and Wu Zhihao were elected as supervisors. Gu Zhenmin was elected as alternate supervisor.

Business Report: At the beginning of the bank's opening, it coincided with the aftermath of the Shanghai war. The business and financial markets were showing signs of decline. Until last year, due to the impact of the US silver policy, credit became extremely tight. As the year was coming to an end, banks and money shops with historical credit were seen clearing, going into liquidation, and collapsing, one after another. However, the bank's business has only been three years old so far. It has been able to stand firm in the midst of stormy waves, dealing with things with ease and steadily overcoming difficulties. This is not only due to the bank's consistent prudent policies and the trust of society, but also to the guidance of the shareholders and the assistance of colleagues. If the market turns better in the future, the development of the bank's business will have hope. This can be told to the shareholders. As the bank's business gradually grew last year, and the receipts and payments became more frequent, the original location on Shanxi Road was not enough to expand the layout. Therefore, a site was selected at No. 510 Nanjing Road, and construction materials were gathered. It was not until December 1st last year that we were able to move in. With convenient transportation and a magnificent foundation, the business has seen great prosperity. At the time of the year-end settlement, the total value of all the bank's assets and the total value of the assets of the savings department's head office and branches were higher than in the previous year. This can be told to the shareholders. At the second session of the third board of directors meeting, the bank resolved to establish a Hangzhou branch and began preparations. It opened in March last year. Although the business hours have only been more than three months, the receipt of various deposits has reached more than 100,000 yuan. If given a considerable period of time, the gradual development of the business is to be expected. This can be told to the shareholders. In view of the fact that each important area of the bank in this port has branches and sub-branches, and the competition in business is very fierce, in order to avoid the heavy and take the light, the bank chose counties and cities in the interior with prosperous commerce to establish sub-offices in order to have more opportunities to serve the rural areas. In view of the fact that Pinghu County in Zhejiang has convenient transportation and wealthy residents, and that in addition to the old-fashioned money shops holding the financial hub, the emerging banking organizations have not yet been established, we chose a site on Dongmen Avenue in the city to establish a Pinghu office at extremely low cost. It started business on April 15 and has been deeply trusted by local people, especially receiving praise from the Pinghu Xinglun community. This can be told to the shareholders. In the future, the bank's operational policy will be to uphold the spirit of steady progress, work hard, and continue to choose inland counties and cities with prosperous commerce that other banks have not yet paid attention to, and gradually establish sub-offices in order to expand the bank's financial network for serving society, so as to live up to the shareholders' expectations.

Ningbo and Dinghai Fellow Countrymen Associations Urgently Request the Ban of Liva Village Pleasure Boats 147

Liva Kurita Village in Western Shanghai, which connects to the public river, provides rowing boats specifically for tourists to enjoy leisurely rides. On the 22nd of this month, Chen Wenlan and Chen Xiufeng, siblings from Dinghai, went to the village for a boat ride and tragically drowned. The details have already been recorded in this newspaper. Now, the Ningbo Association in Shanghai and the Dinghai Association in Shanghai, considering that the village has no life-saving equipment and that it concerns public safety, have sent a letter to the Shanghai Municipal Government and the Municipal Public Security Bureau, requesting them to find a way to ban it. Their original letter is as follows: We humbly inform you that upon reading a news item in this newspaper on the 22nd of this month, entitled "Tragic Rowing Accident at Liva Kurita Village Yesterday," we were shocked to learn that our fellow countrymen Chen Wenlan and Chen Xiufeng had tragically drowned in the village. We immediately sent personnel to Chen's residence to inquire about the situation and rushed to the scene of the accident in the village to investigate. Afterward, we were informed that the rowing boats in the village are about 16 feet long and 7.5 feet wide, with pointed bows and sterns and narrow bottoms. The river at that location is about ten or more zhang wide and over two zhang deep. We have verified that the river is a public river, extending for several li. The section near the village is less than ten zhang, and beyond that, the river flows through open fields. There are no sidewalks or docks along the banks, and there is absolutely no life-saving equipment. At the starting point, there is a sign stating that the fee is one yuan per hour, without boatmen, etc. We have taken films of the sign and the boat's hull and are submitting them for review. We have found that the village provides rowing boats for people to play with, charging as much as one yuan per hour, but not only are there no boatmen, there is also no life-saving equipment, and the river connects far beyond the village, being both wide and deep. In this situation, the village owner is treating human lives as a joke. The dead are gone, but the future is long, and we must take measures to prevent similar incidents from happening again. Therefore, we jointly submit this letter to the Municipal Bureau Chief for your review. We urge you to promptly investigate and strictly ban the operation to avoid future dangers and also request a reply. We believe that after the Municipal Government and the Municipal Public Security Bureau approve the letter, there will certainly be corresponding measures taken to prevent a recurrence of such an event.

A Leading Figure in the Aviation Field, Qin Dajun, Will Return to China Soon 149

Among those in China who study aviation, some only learn to fly, while others only know about machinery. Most have not deeply studied the principles. There are even fewer who are proficient in the principles, enthusiastically study aircraft and motor manufacturing, and also know how to fly. The advanced parts of aviation principles require the application of higher physics and mathematics. It is not easy to understand without a good foundation in mathematics and physics and many years of research in aviation. Now, there is Qin Dajun, from Wuxi, a graduate of the Mathematics, Physics, and Chemistry Department of the former National Nanjing Higher Normal School and a Bachelor of Science from Southeast University. He studied in France and Germany for three years. In France, he graduated from the Paris National Higher Aviation School and obtained a degree in Aviation Engineering from the French Ministry of Aviation. He then obtained a German Engineering Doctorate from the German National Aachen Aviation Research Institute. He interned in aviation factories in France and Germany and visited and surveyed testing laboratories and factories in various European countries. Mr. Qin's honors abroad and his profound practical knowledge are both rare and valuable. It is rare for Chinese people to obtain a French National Aviation Engineer degree in France, and it is also extremely rare to obtain an Engineering Doctorate degree in Germany (an Engineering Doctorate is the most difficult degree to obtain in Germany). Mr. Qin has obtained both. It is truly gratifying that China's aviation field has gained another talent. It is said that Mr. Qin will return to China in mid-May to serve his motherland.

Yu Yongkang Receives a Medical Doctorate 150

The famous doctor Yu Yongkang graduated from the Medical Department of Tongji University in 1928. He then served in the venereal disease and dermatology department and the obstetrics department of Shanghai Baozhen Hospital for six years, treating countless patients. He now has his own clinic at 22 Xiude New Village, Chengdu Road. Based on his clinical experience, he discovered a method for dissipating buboes. His thesis was published in the most famous German medical journal on venereal diseases and dermatology, volume 99, issue 51. As a result, he was awarded a medical doctorate. At the Medical and Natural Science Society meeting on the 27th of this month (the day before yesterday), Dr. Kan Lo, a famous professor from a German university, presented Mr. Yu with his medical doctorate certificate, creating a grand scene for a time.

Overview of the Rose Garden New Village Project 151

The Rose Garden New Village, built by the China New Village Construction Society, has been progressing step by step according to the planned construction stages since construction began on December 9th of last year. It is expected that it can be fully completed within this year. Here is a brief overview of the village's construction:

Residences of All Levels: The ABC-level residences in the village have already started construction, and 60-70% of the entire roofing and interior decoration and partitioning have been completed. The landscaping is now being planned. The residences are surrounded by greenery as fences, creating a quiet and beautiful environment. Seasonal flowers and trees are planted in the courtyard, changing the scenery at any time, making the courtyard and residences complement each other. The foundation and grey-line wall base construction for the DE-level residences has also begun.

Surrounding Walls: Hedges are being built around the village. Steel fences are used as barriers along the Shanghai-Minhang Road, all of which have been completed. Empty space of several inches is left outside the steel fence, planted with evergreen shrubs, forming an outward-sloping or wavy shape. Various colors of climbing roses will be planted at the base of the steel fence to display the unique style of the village.

Road Construction: The section of Shanghai-Minhang Road within the village area has been planted with roadside trees by the society, using large-leaf French plane trees. The base and drainage ditches of the roads within the village have mostly been completed. The construction of the lawns on both sides and the electric poles is planned to begin within the next few days. The road surface is temporarily delayed due to the transport of freight vehicles. French plane trees will be planted as roadside trees on the north-south roads in the village, and German locust trees will be selected for the east-west roads.

River Channel Improvement: The dredging project of the Liuyun River in the village has been completed. The construction of the lawns, sidewalks, electric poles, and mud piers on both sides is also being planned. It is planned to build steel and concrete bridges over the Liuyun River that crosses Boai and Huzu Roads. The bridge on Huzu Road has already started construction. Trees have also begun to be planted on both sides of the river channel, with a mixture of dragon junipers and spherical junipers. Benches will be set up underneath for residents to rest.

Remaining Residences: According to the business department of the society, there are still some residences remaining in the village, including four B-level residences and five D-level residences. Those who love the new village life should purchase them quickly, lest they regret it later. In addition, the society's specially created new village real estate cooperative investment, which takes into account the interests of both homeowners and residents, has been widely sympathized with and praised by all sectors of society. Many people have been going to the agency department at 918 Aidingia Road in recent days to obtain information and discuss investments.

The Children's Work of the Ciyou Orphanage's Boys' Service Corps 152

The Shanghai Buddhist Association's Ciyou Orphanage on Gonghe Xin Road in Zhabei usually pays great attention to work-study programs and healthy living. Recently, in order to cultivate children's ability to serve, they organized a Boys' Service Corps and provided various new training methods, with excellent results. Whenever various groups and ships are recruited for service, they are quite effective in maintaining order. Considering that residents near the orphanage do not pay much attention to cleanliness and hygiene, which is detrimental to public health, the corps leads its members to clean up daily and also posts notices to promote the meaning of the New Life Movement. In recent days, the area near the orphanage has been cleared of all filth, and the atmosphere is completely new, for which the residents are very grateful.

The Weather Turned Cold Yesterday 153

The weather in this city has been alternating between cold and warm, with dense fog. The thermometer had reached above 80 degrees the day before yesterday, and citizens were wearing thin clothing. Yesterday morning, the weather suddenly turned cold, and there was light rain. According to the astronomical observatory, the temperature dropped to 63 degrees, a difference of more than ten degrees. The Huangpu River was shrouded in fog all day, making it difficult to distinguish anything beyond a hundred steps. Citizens are catching colds easily due to the cold and warm weather, especially children. A Pacific hurricane has also emerged. According to weather reports, there is a hurricane stalled east of Luzon Island, and its direction is unclear, but it is not expected to come north.

Continued Report on the Murderer's Prison Break from the Second Special District Court Detention Center 154

Chen Jinlan Planned Her Escape Early, Yang Xingcun and Yan Ling Appear in Court

Chen Jinlan, a murderer detained in the Second Special District Court Detention Center, escaped from prison, implicating the guards on duty. Fang Yuqi was sentenced to two years and six months of imprisonment, and Zhou Wenjin was sentenced to two years of imprisonment. Later, the police arrested Chen and Wang Afu, who lent Chen money for hiding, and escorted them to the Second Special District Court's Criminal Court. The prosecutor and the police department filed public lawsuits against Chen and Wang separately. According to Chen's confession, he escaped around 1:00 AM on the night of December 26th, during the shift of a guard named Yang. This has already been reported in the newspapers. Now, Sun Xionggen, who is concurrently serving as the director of the detention center, based on the time Chen confessed, ordered the guards Yang Xingcun and Yan Ling to be placed under supervision and transferred to the prosecutor's office for investigation and handling. The day before yesterday, Prosecutor Wang Ren, accompanied by Clerk Peng Yi, specially opened Criminal Court No. 2 and ordered Chen, Yang, and Yan to be brought in for questioning. According to Chen Jinlan's confession, he was arrested for a murder case and sentenced to 15 years of imprisonment. After the appeal, the sentence was reduced to 12 years. He felt that this lawsuit was truly unjust, so after the first judgment, he had the intention of escaping. First, he found a half-foot-long piece of lead wire used by prisoners to pick their ears in another room. He usually paid attention to how the guards opened the inner and outer iron doors, which were opened with one key. So, when it was quiet, he made a key. He had already made it a month ago. On the night of December 26th, about two hours after the guards changed shifts, around 1:00 AM, the guard named Yang was running back and forth. He heard the sound of his leather shoes running outside the release room around the corner. He then opened the door and went outside and walked out of the main gate. Yan Ling testified that he was transferred from Caohejing to serve. At the time of Chen's escape, it had only been a little over a month. He did not know Chen. He was in charge of the main gate and also the iron gate. It was a mobile position. If the director and others came in and out, he would have to open the door. He did not see Chen escape. The official said that former Director Gao said that Yan was in charge of the main gate, not a mobile position. Yan replied that he asked to investigate with the people in the office and his colleagues. The director, Bai Zengqing, was also summoned to inquire about Yan Ling's position. Yang Xingcun was not mentioned. According to his confession, when he took over and left the shift, he checked the prisoners in each cell and there were no missing. He was in charge of seven cells. He only discovered Chen's escape when he opened it at 7:00 AM. After the interrogation, the official ordered Chen to be sent back to custody. Yang and Yan returned to the detention center to await further investigation. The court then adjourned.

Robbers Rampage in Luodian Countryside, Zhang Baohua's Entire Family Killed and Injured by Robbers, Shanghai-Taicang Road Long-Distance Telephone Destroyed by Robbers 155

At the home of Zhang Baohua, a farmer in Dongxuliqiao Village, Luodian Town, Baoshan County, around 9:00 PM on the evening of the 26th (the day before yesterday), a large group of over twenty robbers suddenly arrived, each holding iron and wooden sticks, long and short knives, and pistols. At that time, Zhang and his family were all asleep. The robbers pried open the gate and rushed in. Zhang heard the noise and suspected that they were thieves, so he immediately called his family to get up and shout for help. Unexpectedly, this angered the robbers. Knives and sticks were wielded at the same time, striking people indiscriminately, knocking Zhang Baohua's entire family to the ground, bleeding profusely. The robbers saw that they had all fallen to the ground, and then sent several robbers to watch over them. Several robbers guarded the gate, and the rest entered the bedrooms to search. They rummaged through the boxes and cabinets and robbed silver dollars, gold jewelry, etc., worth about 300 yuan, and then left swaggeringly. Later, the injured people were sent to Luodian Hospital for treatment. It was heard that Zhang Baohua was attacked in the head by the robbers, and the injury was extremely serious, and there was a danger to his life. It was also learned that around 10:00 PM that night, the home of Qian Kunxiang, a villager in Dongqian Village in the town, was also robbed in the same way, with greater losses, but no one was injured. Around 11:00 PM on the following day (Saturday), six or seven people suddenly came to the home of Zhu Bingsheng, the station chief of Changbangqiao Station on Shanghai-Taicang Road, also holding iron and wooden sticks, knives and guns. They first destroyed the telephone of the Shanghai-Taicang Long-Distance Bus Company, and then tied up Station Chief Zhu with ropes and searched as they pleased. It is estimated that clothing, silver notes, etc. worth over 100 yuan were robbed. The victims in the above cases have all reported to the Luodian Town Public Security Bureau, requesting them to investigate and pursue the stolen goods and the robbers.

Special Announcement

Traffic Bank Business Report (3) 167

B. Domestic Economic Recession

Now, let's look back at the current state of our country's economy. What is it like? And what is the impact on the banking industry? The exchange rate of silver dollars has naturally shrunk due to the fluctuations in foreign exchange rates. Regarding important matters such as production, prices, and trade, the details are as follows:

(1) The production of major food crops only accounts for 82% of the previous year (estimated by the Central Agricultural Experiment Institute). Although the value of imported foreign rice decreased by approximately 8 million yuan compared to the previous year, wheat also decreased by approximately 5 million yuan, and flour decreased by approximately 2 million yuan, the average index of agricultural products in various regions in the first half of the year was more than 20% lower than the same period last year. The price of flour once fell to around 1.90 yuan per bag.

(2) Although the cotton output is estimated to increase by approximately one million piculs this year compared to the previous year, and the price has improved due to the assistance of banks and cooperatives, the average market price of standard cotton throughout the year is still 7.9 cents lower than the previous year. The value of imported foreign cotton decreased by approximately 8.8 million yuan due to the increase in tariffs.

(3) Due to the reduction in working hours per week in cotton mills nationwide, the output of cotton yarn decreased, and inventory was lower than the previous year. The lowest price once fell to 170 yuan. The average market price of standard yarn throughout the year in Guannei was 19.67 yuan lower than the previous year. The imported quantity is difficult to calculate due to the products of foreign-owned yarn mills in China. However, there is already a committee organized for the control of cotton yarn.

(4) Due to the severe decline in the silk market, most silk mills have suspended operations, resulting in a decrease in both production and sales. The export value decreased by approximately 28 million yuan compared to the previous year. The price of raw silk in the Shanghai foreign exchange market sharply declined, regardless of whether it was yellow, white, upper, or lower grades. In August and September, the average market price of mid-grade mill silk was 460 yuan, a decrease of more than 300 yuan compared to the same period in the tenth year (records from the Raw Silk Export Association). The control of silk cocoons is still in its initial stages.

(5) Due to the severe cold in Anhui, the main tea-producing area, last winter, the tea harvest was very poor, estimated to be only 180,000 piculs. Fortunately, the sales of black tea to the United Kingdom and Russia have rebounded, exports have increased, and the market price is also high. However, the price of green tea has fallen sharply, and foreign sales have also decreased. The statistics for tea exports are approximately 36 million yuan, an increase of approximately 2 million yuan compared to the previous year. Overall, both import and export trade have decreased, but the trade deficit still reached a huge amount of more than 49.4 million yuan.

In summary, production has decreased, prices have fallen, exchange rates have shrunk, and trade is in reverse. The rural economy is on the verge of bankruptcy. The purchasing power of the people has become increasingly weak, leading to a sharp decline in the prosperity of the market. The price of urban real estate has fallen sharply, resulting in increased unemployment and tighter credit. Initially, domestic funds were concentrated in cities, and interbank lending rates were as low as Bai Xie. Subsequently, silver flowed out, and credit became tight, with daily lending rates as high as six cents. Since June, the United States has been buying silver, and the price of silver in Shanghai has often been lower than that in the United Kingdom and the United States. Due to the pursuit of profit, the amount of silver exported was very large. Although the government levied silver taxes, cracked down on speculative bidding, and stipulated measures such as stable exchange rates and stable markets in an attempt to control the situation, the overall effect on the situation was limited. The total silver surplus from the entire country was worth more than 15.59 million silver dollars. At the end of the year, the silver reserves in Shanghai were only more than 25.1 million silver dollars. Including silver ingots and large bars, the total was only approximately 33.5 million yuan, a decrease of 26 million yuan compared to the highest reserve amount this year. With the reserves being depleted and credit becoming tighter, it has led to an extremely tight financial situation in the city. International economic policies are so unfavorable to our country's economy, and the impact on Shanghai's financial industry is so great. The difficulty in coping with the situation is evident. (To be continued)

Spring and Autumn

Snippets 168

— (He Wei)

The more one realizes that people must die, the harder one should strive. Since it is known that this body will inevitably dissolve in the future, wouldn't it be greatly worthwhile to build this dissolving body on beneficial endeavors?

When the ground is muddy during rain, one thinks of how comfortable it will be when the weather is clear. But when the weather is clear, who still thinks of the pain of rain? Greed may be a bad habit in life, but at the same time, it can enable one to build great achievements.

If a person can often think of 'the pain of asking others for help when one has no money' when they are rich, I believe they will certainly not regard money as less important than a feather.

The surface of reality is simple and crude, while the surface of falsehood is beautiful and enviable. Therefore, most people in the world abandon reality and pursue falsehood!

The Dancer Without Fashion 169

— Da Mu

Every weekend evening, we always spend two hours at tea dances. Generally speaking, it is still the cheapest form of entertainment. Three or four familiar friends occupy a small round table in that stimulating room with elegant and natural posture, sitting, drinking strong coffee, tasting delicately woven inlaid pastries, and smoking the cigarettes that one loves and carries in the pocket.

As soon as that "Whistling In the Dark" tune starts, it's like a general mobilization order has been issued. Dance partners bump into each other in the dark. Youngsters whose footwork isn't skilled refuse to miss this session, and those who are obsessed with sensuality also refuse to miss it. The foxtrot has a sense of familiarity, but this session has a more tender and secluded sentiment. My friends all embraced their respective loved ones and blended into the darkness.

Sitting alone, propping my chin up, coldly watching the large whirlpool of men and women in front of me, swirling around and around. However, a girl who was close to the edge of the whirlpool, hanging her head, caught my eye. She was also sitting alone, coldly, just like me. However, she was the seller of stimulation and gentleness, and in such an attractive place, she was still abandoned. Why? I started to wonder, feeling that her loneliness was different from mine, and her deeply furrowed brow probably tasted bitter!

However, my friends refused to forgive her, "What is there that makes people feel powerful? She doesn't even have a relatively eye-catching fashion." Everyone said with a sneer. However, I was fortunate for her, "Fashion saved her body." I silently praised the dancer without fashion.

Rambling Talk on Goldfish 170

— Wu Jiren

I recently received a letter from Mr. Chen Zhelu of Nantai, Fujian, inquiring about the treatment method for goldfish developing white spots. Therefore, based on my limited knowledge, I offer a few suggestions.

The white spots on the fish's body are initially small and indistinguishable, gradually becoming apparent and increasing in number. According to this, these white spots are not generated from within the body, but are a type of bacteria. This can be proven by microscopic examination. They bite into the fish's skin, penetrating deep into the flesh, spreading extremely quickly, and can spread throughout the entire tank in no time. The methods of prevention are: first, isolation, to prevent contact with healthy fish; second, do not change the water, let it remain in the original water, as changing the water will only accelerate their death; third, do not feed, it must be stopped for a long time, only until the fish's illness has completely subsided (no more white spots are seen) and the color has returned (the fish's color fades when ill, lacking its previous luster), can it be fed normally; fourth, expose it to more sunlight. The white spots gradually turn red when exposed to sunlight, and then turn grayish-brown. This is a sign that the bacteria are dying. If the fish is still fed after the illness, the fish's body will be nourished and abundant, and the bacteria will be able to grow even longer, making it not only difficult to treat, but also causing it to spread throughout the body and die. I believe that the methods for treating white spots, in addition to quick isolation, stopping feeding, not changing the water, and more exposure to sunlight, have no other methods.

Why do fish with white spots mostly originate from northern fish bodies? There is also a reason for this. Northern fish are transported south by ship, packed in wooden barrels. The area of the barrel, let's say, can usually hold a hundred fish, but when they are loaded onto the ship, they must put in five or six hundred fish, because they want to have more quantity and take up less space. However, when there are many fish and the container is small, they must float to the surface, so they often add fresh water to regulate it. After many days of travel, the disease has been lurking. When they arrive in Shanghai, they are changed to the water here. At first, they seem very lively, so they are fed normally. Little do they know, after not too long, they will gradually stiffen and die. Some may even last until the new year (fish are transported in winter). Once the peach blossom water rises, almost all northern fish die. The symptoms include growing white spots, and sometimes they also develop rot. Some may not even show any symptoms, but nineteen out of ten cannot escape.

According to the above, it seems that northern fish cannot be transported south. No, that's not true. What is the method? That is, after the fish are transported, place them in a tank and do not feed them throughout the winter. Only after the spring thunder has sounded and it has rained many times can they be fed. If fish are transported like this, they will not only have no white spot disease, but will also be able to adapt to the local climate of the south. Some may ask, won't they become thin and damaged if they are not fed throughout the winter? No, it doesn't matter. Therefore, it is clear that those who purchase northern fish species cannot adapt to the local climate unless they pass through two seasons of cold and heat.

Mr. Chen also inquired that sometimes fish tails grow insects that lie within the mucous membrane, and over time, they bleed. These insects look like earthworms, as thin as a thread, and several inches long. They heal immediately after being removed, and are not harmful. This is called a leech, which is indeed found in Suzhou. They are mostly mixed into the fish tank from water maggots. Pay close attention when feeding and remove them immediately, there is no major problem.

Acknowledgement The third volume, eleventh issue of the Qinghe Magazine, edited by Mr. Chen Gan Yi, was published on schedule on the sixteenth of this month. This magazine is eagerly awaited every month, and it is never late. In addition to the various famous works that have already been published in installments, the content of each manuscript also includes Mr. He Zizhen's diary, Mr. Chen Ziyan's Zunhu Chamber Poetry Talks, Notes from Jingzhaoxuan, Mr. Chen Xie's Yinyuan Poetry Talks Excerpts, Mr. Yang Wuyang's Sea Country Miscellany, Dragonfly Continent Poetry Records, Xia Que'an's drama scripts Gao Tang Dream and Little Zhou Hou, all of which are endlessly enjoyable. The eight characters analyzed by the owner of Kan Yun Lou are published once every other issue, four people each time, and they all talk about subtle truths. The twelfth issue has been sent to print and will be published on the first of next month. The retail price is still 30 cents per copy, and the annual subscription is reduced. There are not many copies left, so those who want to buy should do so quickly. I received a complimentary copy yesterday, and I would like to express my gratitude here.

Presenting Skills for Survival 171

— Juan Yin

The Mists of Imperial Incense Record 172

— Originally written by Princess Der Ling, translated by Qin Shouou

Description of Phoenix Shoes: Almost everything that can be written about shoes has already been written. Now there is only one last point that can be discussed, and that is the relationship between shoes and the seasons. Even the shoes worn by commoners have different categories such as cotton shoes, lined shoes, and gauze shoes, so what about the Empress Dowager? In Chapter Eight of this book, I mentioned that the materials of the clothes in the palace must be changed according to the seasons, and even the flowers embroidered on the clothes have their own regulations. The same is true for shoes, so there is no need to repeat it. I will only talk about the phoenix shoes used by the Empress Dowager in winter. The Empress Dowager certainly does not want to wear heavy cotton shoes, so her shoes are lined with the best silk cotton, and the opening of the shoes is edged with a circle of leather. This circle of leather is naturally made of silver rat or sable.

The artisans employed by the Empress Dowager were all settled behind Longevity Hill, across from Kunming Lake. On this hillside, several palace courtyards of similar sizes were neatly separated, with each courtyard housing artisans of a specific craft, never mixed together. For example, there was a dedicated palace courtyard for those who raised silkworms, and the artisans who made silk also had their own residences and workplaces, and the shoemakers had another place. Although they were very close, they all had their own separate entrances, like several independent factories. Therefore, this part of the Summer Palace can be said to be a small-scale industrial area. The artisans inside were as busy as a swarm of bees all year round. However, all the products here are very different from the products of any factory in China: first, the silk, cocoons, or phoenix shoes needed in the palace are not just one or two types, but often hundreds or thousands of types, and each type does not need to be much, only very exquisite one or two pieces; second, the skills of the artisans in the palace are indeed higher than those of all other workers elsewhere, as a result of on-site comparisons. (302)

Local Customs and Anecdotes

Strolling in Hangzhou 173

— Wang Geda

I often say that Zhou Shixun is our most interesting leader because even a joke from his flexible mouth contains philosophy or psychology. From our trip to Hangzhou this time, I am even more convinced that there is no exaggeration in my words.

When our group reached the middle of the Nine Creeks and Eighteen Streams, Shidong's witty remarks began, he said, friends! "Do you know? Hangzhou is made up of three types of people, one is "dead people," one is "half-dead people," and one is "living people." Only with dead people can there be "chastity archways, tombs, and ancestral halls." Only with half-dead people can there be "forests, temples, churches, and monasteries." Only with living people can there be "spring outings, pilgrimages, and Buddhist worship." If one of the three is missing, it cannot be Hangzhou." We certainly couldn't find a better reason to deny it, and followed our leader forward amid a chorus of "yes" sounds.

Shixun has a tea addiction, so he took our group to Lian'an Temple. Although the tea here is not as famous as Hupao, the source of the water is one into two and two into one, and the environment is indeed more secluded than Hupao, especially the Nan forests standing respectfully in a line to greet you, which make people linger. When we entered the temple, a receptionist came to greet us. Of course, we had to comment on the fragrant tea here, especially since we were already parched to the extreme. At this time, Shixun continued to talk about the psychology of using a cane in Hangzhou, which was another interesting conversation and worth using as a guide to Hangzhou.

He said, "When people arrive in Hangzhou, in order to achieve their goal of visiting the mountains, as soon as they arrive in Hangzhou, they think that they must prepare a cane in advance, because with it, they can help people when visiting the mountains. In fact, those who secretly take canes have suffered a lot of losses, while the general merchants, peddlers, rickshaw pullers, and boatmen of Hangzhou have gained what they call the "peak season." If you don't believe me, you can try it. If you walk on the lakeside with a cane, there will immediately be a group of rickshaw pullers and boatmen following closely behind you, reciting their slogan-like itineraries, "Sir, do you want a car (or boat) to Lingyin, Hupao, Three Tianzhu, Nine Creeks and Eighteen Streams, Yellow Dragon Cave, Yixia Cave, cheaper price, do you want it?" If you don't firmly say no, they may follow you for more than half a kilometer. If you offer them a price, then you have to continue to be careful that your clothes are not torn apart by their pulling and tearing. As a result, the price you offer, if it is ever agreed upon, will always be more expensive than if you didn't take a cane.

If you are walking on the streets, then the shop assistants, who rely on the one spring for the three winter period, will come up to you and say, "Sir, do you want to buy some fragrant baskets, Buddhist beads, West Lake lotus root powder, fragrant torreya seeds?" If the deal is made, it will also be more expensive than if you didn't take a cane.

In short, the cane in Hangzhou is indeed enough to help people travel, and it is also a trademark for Hangzhou people to field to foreign tourists. On the surface, they are particularly attentive to those who carry canes, but in reality, they want you to lose more, because in Hangzhou, Hangzhou people, or outsiders who have lived in Hangzhou for a long time, except for a few old and frail old men, do not carry canes. Otherwise, you only see three legs on the road all year round. Everything in the world has its advantages and disadvantages. The cane in Hangzhou is one of them." Shixun's words gave us another good lesson for traveling in Hangzhou.

Little Western Paradise 174

— Written by Zhang Henshui

Chapter Twelve Ashamed of Not Having Clothes, Hanging Curtains to Avoid Hardships, Saving Candles, Copying Paintings at Dawn

Cheng Zhiqian said: "In that case, you are a passionate educator. I have a few questions about education in the Northwest that I'd like to discuss with you, old brother. Would you be willing to enlighten me?" These two sentences piqued You Ke's interest, and he didn't want to tutor Bei Hai anymore. The two of them were sitting on opposite sides of the table. He dragged his chair to sit in front of him, rolled up his sleeves, and said, "I can't say 'enlighten me', let's research together. Mr. Cheng has come here to investigate education, why don't you tell me your thoughts first?" Zhiqian said: "It would be too long to talk about the entire education system. Let's talk about a few interesting questions. I went west, all the way to Qinghai and Ningxia. Of course, there's no education to speak of in those places. Let's just say that two or three hundred miles away to the west, I arrived at a county town. This county is very desolate. Standing at a high place, you can see all the rooftops of the houses at a glance, and count them off. But after all, it's a county town, so there must be a school. Outside the gate of an ancient temple, the temple plaque had been removed, and like in the East, there was a school plaque with white characters on a blue background, reading 'Zunzhe County First Elementary School'. At that time, I went inside to visit, and at the temple gate I met a man around thirty years old, wearing a blue cloth jacket and pants, with quite a few ink stains on his body. His head was shaved, without a braid or long hair on the side of his neck. Here, it was determined that he was a student. I said to him, 'I'm here to visit, are you a teacher here?' But his answer was beyond my expectations, he was actually a student here. I also know that students in the Northwest can't be judged by age, but to have such a large age difference was something I didn't believe before I came here." (192)

This demonstrates the efforts of Sino-Polish members in bridging the cultures of the two countries and is highly admirable. Chinese culture has a long history. Since the era of Emperors Tang and Yu, there has been construction in politics, philosophy, humanities, education, etc. Unfortunately, in later times, people only knew how to worship the ancients and failed to pay attention to innovation, resulting in many shortcomings. During the time of Zeng Wengong, Li Hongzhang, Zhang Zhidong, and others in the late Qing Dynasty, there was already a trend of accepting Western culture. Mr. Sun Yat-sen advocated using scientific methods to organize and promote China's inherent culture and to absorb Western culture in a way that suits the national conditions, which we can use as a guideline. Poland is an emerging country whose artistic expression and political development can be used as a reference for us. The bridging of Sino-Polish culture is worthy of everyone's efforts. Wang Shijie, the representative of the Ministry of Education, then delivered an inquiry, briefly stating that the Sino-Polish Cultural Association has been established for two years. In the past, due to the efforts of each member in working during their busy schedules, much has been done to introduce Sino-Polish culture, and publications have been printed. It is the humble opinion that the union between peoples and nations can be achieved through political, commercial, economic, and cultural aspects. Political unions can often be realized in a very short time through the promotion of influential figures. Unions from commercial and economic aspects also take a short time. However, cultural unions are more difficult and cannot be achieved in a short time. It is necessary to have the majority of people in both countries understand each other, and from understanding to respect, and only with respect can there be close cooperation. Therefore, the time is long, and the matter is complicated. Therefore, it is hoped that the colleagues in this association will work together and recognize that bridging Sino-Polish culture is a permanent or lifelong task. If this is promoted, then nations and nations can understand, respect, and unite with each other.

The reason why he was able to deeply understand the situation in China during the three and a half years he was in China was largely due to the help of Chinese friends and members of this association. Serving in the transportation sector in China, he felt that Chinese culture had paid attention to transportation as early as 4,000 years ago, especially during the Han Dynasty. Various regions were able to seek practicality based on local needs. The introduction of modern transportation tools was also the result of the Chinese people's own construction efforts. After all, 800 million Chinese people rely on transportation to make a living, so they have to seek adaptation in order to make a living. The speed of modern progress in China may require more time in other countries. He will be leaving China this time after a long time in China. After leaving, he will let the world know the achievements of China's construction efforts. Even in ordinary life, the Chinese principles of propriety, righteousness, integrity, and shame are moral principles that can be adopted by all countries in the world. He has been with everyone for a long time and firmly believes that the bridging of Sino-Polish culture will be successful.

The details are recorded as follows:

Attending Representatives: Those present yesterday included Director Pan and Section Chief Jiang of the Municipal Education Bureau, members of the Opera Review Committee, Lü Hailan, Ding Shoutang, Xu Gongwan, Yuan Zengyu, Sun Yucai, Cheng Fengxiang, Peng Quji, as well as representatives from the Shanghai Opera Research Association, the Su Opera Research Association, the Huaji Opera Research Association, the Runyu Society Pingtan Research Association, the Guangyu Society, the Siming Opera Research Association, the Yongyu Society Shanghai Storytelling Research Association, the Weiyang Pinghua Improvement Association, and more than 100 representatives from various drama troupes such as Tianyunlou, Sun Sun Amusement Park, New World, and Fu'an Amusement Park.

Director's Report: Chairman Director Pan reported in brief that the Municipal Education Bureau had invited all personnel from Shanghai's performing arts circles here today to hold a symposium, on the one hand, to discuss improving the performing arts, and on the other hand, to ask everyone to support the literacy movement organized by the city. As everyone knows, the current national environment is becoming increasingly dangerous. To save China, all the people of the country must work together. But to make all the people of the country save the country, they must first understand the danger of the country and the importance of saving the country. To make them understand, in addition to using direct conversations to instruct them, in order to be universally effective, it is necessary to rely on writing. In the past, more than 80% of the Chinese people were illiterate. In recent years, there has been more progress, but still more than 70% are illiterate, with an estimated 300 million or more people being illiterate. How to make them know the country?

Situations in Various Countries: The strength, wealth, and poverty of a country are closely related to literacy. 97% of the Japanese people are literate, so they can become a strong country. Literacy is the foundation of civilization in a country. The citizens of the United Kingdom, the United States, and France are mostly literate. Soviet Russia and Turkey also had more than 80% illiteracy in the past, but since the end of the European War, only seventeen years of effort have resulted in more than 80% of the people being literate. Therefore, Russia's current national power is very different from before, and Turkey has now become an emerging country, erasing the shame of being called the "sick man of the Near East." China has been in revolution for twenty-four years since the revolution, but even if our literate people have made progress, it is only about 10%. According to this proportion, it is not known how many years and months it will take to make more than 80% of the people literate. However, the international situation cannot allow us to wait any longer. We must think of a fast way to make illiterate people literate in the shortest possible time.

Literacy Movement: Therefore, the central government stipulated seven national salvation movements a few years ago, and the first is the literacy movement, which shows its importance. But it must be done by everyone to be achieved. Therefore, all localities are now promoting the literacy movement. The literacy movement in Shanghai is now being carried out on a large scale and permanently in cooperation with the municipal government, party departments at all levels, agencies, and groups. The municipal government allocates funds to run literacy schools, forcing illiterate people to enroll in the school, reading for two months can recognize 600 to 700 characters, reading for one hour a day, without hindering their work time, free of charge, and books are given away. These literacy schools total about 200, each school has six classes, each class has 50 people, teaching for six hours, totaling 300 people. 200 schools have 60,000 people. Graduates every two months, 360,000 people in twelve months. In this way, after one year, illiterate people can recognize 600 characters. We are compiling a reading material based on these 600 characters, gradually incorporating other new characters, so that they can progress day by day.

Expand Propaganda: This campaign will begin on July 1 this year, but before July 1, we must first make everyone in Shanghai, regardless of men, women, old or young, know that illiterate people are willing to come to study and literate people are willing to come to help. Therefore, there is extensive official propaganda, and it is hoped that everyone in the performing arts circles will do their best to help. The current literacy movement propaganda week runs from May 1st to May 7th. During these seven days, whenever and wherever you have the opportunity to perform or speak, try to insert the meaning of literacy as much as possible. This is helping the country, and May 2nd is designated as Electric Broadcast Propaganda Day. The Broadcasting Industry Association has designated China-West Radio Station to broadcast literacy propaganda programs on this day, and other radio stations will also rebroadcast this program. May 4th is Performing Arts Propaganda Day. On this day, all performing arts personnel in the city will be fully mobilized to promote. The Literacy Education Committee has formulated an outline for everyone to refer to, to make illiterate people willing to become literate and literate people willing to teach illiterate people and not be intellectual slaves. It is hoped that everyone can do their best, which is truly a blessing for the country and the nation.

Secondary School Normal Education Industry Research Association Test Committee to Hold Second Meeting Today 184

2 PM at the Lake Society on Guizhou Road

The first meetings of the various groups of the Municipal Secondary School Normal Education Research Association were held separately last week. The second meeting will be held this week. Today is the second meeting of the graduation examination committee at 2 p.m. at the Lake Society on Guizhou Road to discuss whether to change the calculation and disclosure methods of school examination results and the issue of abolishing the examination. The proposals are recorded below: The proposal to suggest that the government expedite the establishment of a national examination to improve national education and implement educational salvation for national salvation will be submitted to the general assembly for discussion (proposer: Minzhi Elementary School). We humbly believe that the past provincial and municipal examinations have been managed separately, with differences in the strictness of test questions and seals, different methods, and different results. It is difficult to unify the level of education and it is not easy to distinguish between the superior and inferior. Therefore, in order to implement the national education improvement policy and improve overall planning in order to control it, a national examination should be expedited. Secondly, if the examination policies are inconsistent, it is difficult to investigate which of the outstanding talents who have been selected in each session are in which place, who they are, how many there are, and what their level is. It is difficult to investigate the great size of the country. The country has no way to reward and cultivate them in order to store up resources for national salvation. If a national examination can be held, the selected and distinguished people can be treated with special courtesy and cultivated through government funding. Military training and education can be carried out in conjunction with each other, and the wise and brave who are selected can serve the country together to complete the revolution and revive the nation. Therefore, in order to implement educational salvation, a national examination should be expedited. Thirdly, there are many subjects, which have already been mentally taxing, and the scope is too broad, making exploration even more difficult, causing students to spend a long time preparing, suffering and searching blindly. Students with weaker bodies often get sick before the test, miss all or part of the test, and are unable to graduate, or get sick and miss classes before the test, and cannot prepare urgently after the illness, resulting in failure. Also, there are often hereditary diseases, which can cause nervous disorders and incurable diseases due to excessive use of the brain, which is harmful. If a national examination can be held, there will be a prescribed scope, and students will not need to waste their brains on preparations outside the prescribed scope. Therefore, for the sake of students' health and development, a national examination should be expedited. Fourthly, the books used in different places and schools are different, and there are many subjects and a wide range, making it difficult for teachers and students to teach and learn. Moreover, there are many kinds of reference books for each subject, with varying degrees of detail, making students sigh with hope and have no idea where to start. Teachers have difficulty finding a basis for selecting supplementary teaching materials, and guidance is therefore uncertain, and it is difficult to avoid the criticism of blind men riding blind horses. Therefore, in order to avoid wasting time and energy for teachers and students in middle schools across the country, to put teaching and learning on the right track, to achieve national unity, and to increase efficiency, a national examination should be expedited. As for the method of national examination, as far as we can see, one is that the teaching materials are nationally fixed, and the textbooks are edited and distributed by the central government or the Ministry of Education and sold in bookstores, or they are selected by the state and uniformly adopted throughout the country, or the examination outlines of various subjects are compiled and printed by the Suzhou Education Bureau, so that the national education control policy can be implemented, the academic thinking of students can be summarized, and the disadvantages of having no standard range can be avoided, and the benefits of achieving twice the result with half the effort can be achieved. Second, the examination administration should be unified, and the national examination of each subject should be held on the same day at the same time. The test questions should be prepared by the Examination Yuan and the Ministry of Education, and the whole country should be unified. Third, the security should be strict, and the proctors should be dispatched by the Yuan and the Ministry, and the examiners should be transferred from various provinces and cities to avoid them. Finally, the Ministry of Education should sum up the examination questions and test papers, and the highest party and government officials of the central government and various provinces and cities should follow the bank's management method to jointly open and close them to show solemnity. The examination room should be extremely solemn to avoid cheating and unfairness. Fourth, the school spirit should be changed to innovation. The national examination questions should be raised and increased as much as possible within the possible range. In addition to setting the minimum standard for ordinary passing grades, the degree to which they exceed them should not be limited so that students with excellent grades can fully express their knowledge, just as there are records and new records in sports, so that students in various provinces and cities can strive to make progress and compete for championships. Not only will the academic level be invisibly improved, but the national school spirit will also be greatly changed, washing away the current abundance of stagnation, negativity, decline, and licentiousness. Fifth, rewards and prevention of abuses. Outstanding graduates who have been selected through the national examination should be sent to national, provincial, and municipal schools or famous private schools with corresponding subjects, and all tuition, food, accommodation, and travel expenses should be waived so that they can further their studies and be stored for national use. Also, students who have passed the national examination should be given a transcript, and they should only be selected for any school based on the examination results, and they should not be allowed to take the examination again. After the implementation of the national examination, the enrollment of all national, provincial, and municipal public schools should be announced and reported at the same time. All lists of admitted and unadmitted students should be reported in order to prevent the abuse of taking non-talented people and to achieve the benefit of equal educational opportunities for the country. Academic and practical skills should be given equal importance, and the tests for various subjects should also include experiments, dissections, surveying, and technical skills in order to avoid overemphasizing academic theory and being impractical. Too much use of the brain will lead to imbalance and hinder health. The above-mentioned reasons and methods for the government to expedite the examination, whether it is appropriate, please make a public decision, which is really convenient for the public.

The Chinese and Portuguese teams, who met in this year's All China Cup football tournament, met again yesterday at Zhongyuan for the first match of this year's China-Portugal Cup. Although they adjusted their troops and tried their best to defend, it was too late to recover, and China won 5-3 in the end. Due to the cloudy weather, there were about 4,000 to 5,000 spectators.
