Writing continuously, I have felt that it has taken a lot of words. To sum it up in a few words, let's come to an end.

(1) China, where toxic fog is permeating, really needs a fairy pill-like elixir to quit smoking, especially a comfortable prescription for smokers.

(2) Egg yolk lecithin is one of many smoking cessation methods. Compared with other methods, it seems very convenient and some people can limit their smoking without necessarily being hospitalized. It is best to use it as an adjunct to other methods, but it does not have the miraculous effect of a fairy pill.

(3) For the sake of the whole country, if more smoking cessation centers are established, many foreign successful methods can be adopted.

(4) Whether or not a drug is effective depends entirely on whether it is used properly. If it is not used properly, it cannot be attributed to the drug.

(5) Good medicine tastes bitter but is beneficial to the disease. Even if the medicine is good, the person taking it must endure a little. If the smoker is unwilling to give up the comfort of smoking at all, mothers will still smoke opium, because, strictly speaking, even the effects of opium and morphine are different.

(6) Increasing the determination of addicts across the country will increase the efficiency of smoking cessation methods. Only with strict laws.

(7) A part of the industry does not conduct much research on the emergence of this egg yolk lecithin, which seems too cold. It seems too early for the Department of Health to issue egg yolk lecithin to solicit statistics, not starting from various doctors and hospitals, but directly selling it to smokers. It is even earlier for pharmaceutical companies to rush to do speculative business before there are many statistics. And it is too bad to use only the words "egg yolk lecithin" to advertise smoking cessation specialists. (End)

Common Sense Q&A About Diseases 212

— Cheng Hanzhang

(56) Rickets (Rachitis) (Continued)

(Question) What kind of symptoms appear in the joints after suffering from rickets?

(Answer) The joints have an abnormally strong range of motion.

(Question) Does rickets occur in older people?

(Answer) Children between the ages of ten and eighteen also develop the same symptoms as infantile rickets; this is specifically called late-onset or adolescent rickets.

(Question) What are the causes of late-onset rickets?

(Answer) It is probably a recurrence of early-onset rickets, so the causes are the same as those of early-onset rickets. But there are also cases where this disease occurs suddenly.

(Question) What are the symptoms of late-onset rickets?

(Answer) At the beginning of this disease, the patient complains of pain when standing or walking, complains of pain, is easily fatigued, and often develops convulsions.

(Question) What happens later?

(Answer) Later, spinal curvature, upper and lower limb curvature, and chest curvature appear. The skull also undergoes characteristic changes, such as a protruding upper chest, skull deformation, pale complexion, muscle relaxation, and delayed development. The limbs gradually shorten, becoming dwarfism.

(Question) How much time passes after the onset of rickets?

(Answer) After several months to several years, it is easy to recur.

(Question) What are the dangerous signs combined with severe rickets?

(Answer) It is often combined with spasmophilia, and sometimes it is easy to cause pyloric spasm, which is very dangerous.

(Question) What is the prognosis of adult rickets?

(Answer) If this disease can be treated properly, most cases can be cured. However, the deformation of the chest and the curvature of the limbs are permanent. In severe cases, development is inhibited, and many become dwarfs.

(Question) What diseases should be differentiated in diagnosis?

(Answer) It should be differentiated from congenital syphilis, Meller-Barlow's disease, and infantile myxedema.

(Question) What are the methods for treating rickets?

(Answer) There are three types of treatments: nutritional therapy, radiation therapy, and vitamin therapy.

(Question) What is nutritional therapy?

(Answer) In infants, breastfeeding should be given. After the child is six months old, add some vegetable juice, broth, fruit juice, etc. to the milk.

(Question) What is radiation therapy?

(Answer) Because the ultraviolet rays in sunlight have a special effect on rickets, patients should be irradiated with artificial sunlight lamps every day, and the cure is very rapid. In addition, the food that patients eat, such as milk and eggs, should also be irradiated with artificial sunlight lamps before eating.

(Question) What is vitamin therapy?

(Answer) It is a method of using supplemental Vitamin D. Cod liver oil contains a lot of Vitamin D and can be taken regularly. In addition, there are pure preparations such as Vanigtol Calciferrol Vitamin-D, etc., which are very effective when taken together with calcium agents. End

Common Sense of Hygiene for Ear, Nose, Throat and Eyes 213

— Tang Renjin

(45) Nasal Obstruction

Nasal obstruction is a major symptom in nasal diseases. Everyone can encounter this symptom because there are too many opportunities for nasal obstruction to occur. All kinds of rhinitis, nasal cavity tumors, nasal septum deformities, and nasal cavity foreign bodies that can cause swelling and thickening of the nasal mucosa can cause nasal obstruction. When we engage in respiratory movements, we mainly rely on the nasal cavity. If there is nasal obstruction, then the nasal cavity is obstructed and not open. The amount of breathing is also insufficient. It is bound to open the mouth to make up for breathing. This is called oral breathing. In cases of severe nasal obstruction, nasal breathing can be completely abandoned. At the same time, the surrounding organs and physical development of the patient are greatly affected by this. The conditions caused by the influence are briefly described as follows.

1. The conditions that occur in the surrounding organs that are most easily affected and develop lesions are the respiratory system and the auditory system. In terms of the respiratory system, pharyngitis, laryngitis, and tracheitis often occur. This is because the air inhaled through oral breathing is mostly dry. It is not like the air inhaled through nasal breathing, which can be moistened by the nasal mucosa, turning it into moist air, so that inflammation of the respiratory organs does not occur. In terms of the auditory system, oral breathing often leads to insufficient ventilation of the Eustachian tube, or even complete blockage. At this time, middle ear diseases are most likely to occur, and deafness often follows. In addition, it should be noted that patients with nasal obstruction often have narrow noises when engaging in nasal breathing. During sleep, snoring often occurs. Sometimes it often causes headaches, nasal attention deficit disorder, memory loss, sleep deprivation and other neurological symptoms.

2. The conditions that occur on physical development In the teenage years, it is the period of development of various parts of the body. If nasal obstruction is suffered during this period, it is easy to cause various developmental obstacles. One of the most prominent types of nasal obstruction that easily causes physical development disorders during adolescence is nasal obstruction caused by adenoid hypertrophy. The reasons for the development of adenoid hypertrophy and the cause of nasal obstruction will be discussed in my next continuation.

Medical Science of Pain Relief (XII) 214

— Li Xing

Angina Pectoris

Angina pectoris is a severe pain that occurs in the heart and radiates to the left shoulder and left arm. At the same time, the condition is critical and has the potential to cause death. The cause of this problem is generally arteriosclerosis of the heart vessels, myocardial degeneration, or problems with the root of the aorta. Syphilis, gout, chronic nephritis, excessive smoking, etc. Angina pectoris attacks are often caused by the use of muscle strength, such as climbing, walking against the wind, or stimulation of the heart and brain, or indigestion in the gastrointestinal tract.

Angina pectoris often strikes suddenly like a bolt from the blue. The heart pain is like a knife stabbing, and at the same time, it radiates to the left shoulder, left arm, and left hand. Each pain attack lasts for several seconds, several minutes, or several hours. Sometimes it occurs repeatedly within a few days, and sometimes it occurs once every few weeks or months. After the pain, the patient feels exhausted for several hours or days. The longer the angina pectoris attack lasts, the more mental loss there is.

When a person has this disease, his life and death are uncertain. Sometimes death occurs during the first attack, sometimes death occurs during the second or third attack, or death occurs at an unknown attack. Some people live for several years despite repeated attacks. In short, the more frequent the pain attacks and the longer they last, the easier it is to die.

The method of relieving angina pectoris can be divided into two types: symptomatic treatment and fundamental treatment. The purpose of symptomatic treatment is to relieve pain temporarily without asking what the cause is. For mild and short-term pain, inhaling amyl nitrite can stop the pain. If it cannot be stopped, injection of painkillers or inhalation of chloroform must be guided by a doctor. The fundamental treatment methods are: (1) Prevention. When the patient is not in pain, pay attention to a quiet life. Do not use physical strength, and do not be stimulated mentally. Be sure to abstain from smoking and drinking. Do not drink strong tea, because the caffeine in tea is stimulating. (2) Treatment. If the patient has had syphilis many years ago, be sure to treat the syphilis seriously. There is still hope for a full recovery from angina pectoris caused by old syphilis if treated properly. There is little certainty of a full recovery from any other type of angina pectoris treatment. In addition to temporary emergency relief, ordinary methods for treating heart disease can also be followed.

Rheumatism

Rheumatism is a disease in which the patient initially develops fever and pain in several joints at the same time, or the heart also becomes inflamed. The cause of the disease is mostly due to chronic inflammation of the tonsils, pyorrhea alveolaris, purulent rhinitis, etc. This kind of joint pain is when the affected joints are inflamed and painful together. It is most commonly found in large joints, such as the knee joint, ankle joint, shoulder joints, elbow joint, etc. The same problem can also occur in any other joint on the body. It is also common for this joint to just get better and other joints to start hurting again. Even a single joint sometimes gets better and sometimes hurts. The joint pain is unbearable day and night, and it is worse at night. The pain is lighter when the patient is lying still, and moving even slightly causes unbearable pain. The above is a summary of the pathology and symptoms of rheumatism. (To be continued)

A Brief Discussion on Pulmonary Tuberculosis (49) 215

— Hu Jiayan

Chapter 11 Complications of Pulmonary Tuberculosis by Mori Nagata Kenji

In general, every disease, in its entire course, will affect other organs due to the spread of symptoms: as a result, the organs there will also develop diseases. This kind of disease is medically called: "complications" or "after-effects." Its occurrence is possible in almost every disease; it is especially common in acute infectious diseases. For example, typhoid fever causes intestinal bleeding and intestinal perforation, as well as perforating peritonitis; scarlet fever causes nephritis and otitis media; measles causes tracheobronchial pneumonia; dysentery causes liver abscesses, etc. When a disease develops complications, its situation is mostly more serious and easily falls into incurability: even when the original disease is in a state of decline or remission, the occurrence of complications causes the patient to return to an extremely serious state. Therefore, in addition to treating the original disease, the physician's diagnosis also involves preventing complications, which is a very important task. Pulmonary tuberculosis is a very complex disease, and its symptoms are almost all-encompassing. Naturally, it cannot be an exception. As for the importance of the relationship between the presence or absence of its complications and the future of the disease, that goes without saying.

Regarding the complications of pulmonary tuberculosis, according to the different organs it affects, it can be divided into the following categories; namely! (1) tuberculous meningitis; (2) pleurisy; (3) pneumothorax; (4) digestive organs; (5) respiratory organs; (6) renal tuberculosis; (7) other complications; (8) the combination of pulmonary tuberculosis and other diseases. Each of these categories has its own special circumstances; now let us describe them one by one below: (To be continued)

Trial of the Beijing Romance Murder Case Begins 216

— Chen

Liu Jinggui of Beiping shot his rival in love, the lover of the popular athlete Lu Ming, and then surrendered himself to the authorities. This has already been a sensational event known to everyone, young and old, and there is no need to repeat it. Here, we want to talk about the trial of this romance murder case.

According to reports, when the trial began, the court deployed a large number of police and soldiers, armed and on guard, like the serious interrogation of Taibao A Shu back then; and the crowd of spectators in front of the court was the largest since the Tao Sijin love murder case. What we pay the most attention to is the situation of the news reporters regarding Liu Jinggui and Lu Ming, who were both defendants, when they were "prisoners." It is said that Liu Jinggui "had a smiling face," while Lu Ming "was sad and drooped his head," which shows that one was seeking benevolence and getting benevolence, regarding death as homecoming, while the other was blaming himself and being extremely embarrassed. Later, Liu confessed that she had physical relations with Lu Ming in Tianshou Apartments in Beiping, Beijing Hotel, Zhangyuan, etc., saying that Lu said, "Everything I have belongs to you, and everything you have belongs to me, what's wrong with sleeping together," which is no different from reading the beautiful articles of the Peony Pavilion. When she confessed that Lu had proposed to dissolve the engagement, she shed tears like rain, which is no different from reading Yuan Ji's Yingying poetry, with a dark and vivid expression.

We have read many of these realistic articles in recent years. For the average poet of self-sacrifice, he or she can probably chant some touching and tear-jerking poems, but we are really "numbed and injured," and can only calmly send a sad elegy. Yes, we admit that in recent years, many young men and women have suffered wounds from the "arrow of the god of love" and died. There are objective reasons for this, but many young men and women forget to avoid reality and hide in the small world of "love," becoming entangled and making it the only true meaning of life. It must be said that this is self-inflicted suffering and making a cocoon to trap oneself.

With the doctrine of love above all else, there have naturally been countless suicides for love and love murders in recent years. This phenomenon, discovered in times of peace, already shows a kind of unhealthy social consciousness, but it is prevalent in modern China, which is so-called "national crisis" and "national crisis," and it is inevitably very uncoordinated. In the present, is the "love" between men and women really like the popular "love classics" say, love is life, love is life, love is the God who dominates everything? It really only makes people sigh!

Liu Jinggui surrendered herself without fear of guilt after killing her rival in love, which shows her courage to "enter the gate of determination." She also showed her "generous righteousness" in "dying for love" by having a "smiling face" when she was interrogated. When she confessed that Lu Ming was ungrateful and terminated the contract, she "shed tears like rain," which can also show her "deep love and deep hatred" for Lu Ming. This kind of "love" spirit can certainly cater to the tastes of the average young master and young lady, scolding Lu Ming several times as "ungrateful." However, if this trend continues, the crime is not that they have nothing to say to society, but that it affects people's escape from reality and a kind of paralysis of "dying for love."

Returning to My Hometown 217

— Erlang

The people of Pengjia Village, nestled in the valley, knew little of the outside world. For two or three hundred years, only one scholar, Peng Guozhu, had emerged from the surrounding villages, which was considered remarkable at the time. Now, they heard that although the Republic no longer had scholars, university students were dozens of times more important than scholars. The son of the scholar was a university student in the capital, which was an incredible honor and glory. When the scholar's son, Peng Yaoxian, was admitted to a university in the capital, the entire Pengjia Village went wild. They set off firecrackers for an entire day, and the ancestral hall was opened wide. The scholar, leading all the elders and children of the clan, paid their respects and sacrifices to the ancestral tablets. Afterwards, they accepted congratulatory gifts of eggs from the neighbors and celebrated all day long. This time, the university student was returning home for a visit. It was said to be a summer vacation, just like a top scholar returning home in an opera. Several days before, the scholar had announced this news, and everyone had been discussing it animatedly, overjoyed and eagerly awaiting the spectacle. Early this morning, some people went up to the hilltop to watch the main road, but it was truly exasperating. After noon, there was still no sign of anything on the road. Everyone believed that a university student's return home for a visit would be a grand affair, with drums beating and escorts shouting, and his official sedan chair would be visible and audible from afar. However, there was no official sedan chair and no sound of drums on the road. Gradually, people became tired, and some went back to the fields.

At dusk, someone rushed down the hillside to the entrance of the village very quickly, it was A'da, Peng's family's long-term worker. A'da running down the hill meant the university student had returned, so everyone rushed to the ancestral hall to congratulate the scholar. Some even brought congratulatory gifts of eggs with them. Before long, they really heard the sound of drums on the hilltop, and then they saw an official sedan chair made of blue wool from afar, with a large white banner in front, followed by a team of armed soldiers after the white banner. "He's here! He's here! "The university student is even more impressive than a top scholar, with soldiers shouting ahead of the sedan chair!" The people of Pengjia Village laughed and shouted.

It turned out that this was all the scholar's idea. Yesterday, he had sent someone to the city to wait for his son and instructed him to ask the county magistrate to send a team to protect him, saying that bandits were rampant on the road. He also told him to make a large banner with the eight characters "Peking University Student Peng Yaoxian" written on it, and the drum players were hired from the city. - How impressive was the university student's return home for a visit? As soon as he entered the village entrance, firecrackers were set off, and the sound of drums echoed all the way to the ancestral hall. The official sedan chair stopped at the entrance of the ancestral hall. The university student was wearing a straw hat, a Western suit, and leather shoes, which was even more remarkable. However, when paying respects and sacrifices to the ancestral tablets, everyone knelt down, but the university student stood and bowed. It was outrageous! Not kneeling down to worship the ancestors, what kind of decorum was that? The scholar was so angry that his face turned red, and the clansmen were discussing it in secret.

However, afterwards, the scholar told people: "Now is the Republican era, kneeling is no longer in vogue. When university students meet the President in the capital, they simply bow." This restored the university student's respect in the eyes of the clansmen.

A Floating World Scene in May 218

— Xu Xizhen

(The sun quietly shines on the faded cherry blossoms lingering on the surface of the stream. Plums are already showing their faces on the branches, green and vibrant. The season bravely and unreservedly strides forward. When the azaleas stand at the end of spring and call out a lamenting cry or two, the times have long lost the leisure of a poet's sigh and lament. Instead, like a valiant warrior, they rush headlong into a hotter, more exciting season without hesitation. The fully grown leaves on the branches are as plump and green as if they have been oiled. The flowers, following the will of nature, donate their beauty in anticipation of the fruits that are not far off. The stagnant water in the small river also resolutely abandons daydreams and doubts, flowing with a natural sense of survival. Here, all the elements of nature: the mountains, the water, the trees, the wild grasses, and the fruits and flowers, just like the will of all human beings in the world, are starting to play the symphony of nature's diligent and arduous construction with a vivid posture. What is blowing here is the wind of May - May, a season that is younger, more upward, and more full of growth than spring.)

No matter how heavy the shadow of hunger and suffering casts over the human world, sighing and madness are absent here, in the natural world, which serves as a barometer of the seasons. There is only an irreversible, unshakable rhythm following nature's will (just as mankind follows the laws of history): They act, they endure, they spend this boiling, scorching summer with a posture of survival, and they walk into a more stable harvest season through labor.

And now: The warm and peaceful climate has followed spring and gone, gradually, finally becoming a black shadow in history. The sweltering summer is not suitable for shallow lingering thoughts, it is full of a terrifying, unstoppable force of growth.

The tune of late April gradually breaks free from comfort. The busy streets are covered with a stubborn, fiery sun that scorches people's hearts. In the midst of this, people ignore the colorful banners of summer sales in the stores, ignore the thin clothes of leisurely women, and just hurry along the sides of the street: Each person carries a restless heart, a grimy body, walking like a tired ox.

Merchants are anxiously beginning to make semi-prayerful hopes: The end of April in this depressed year is a worrisome juncture: But maybe there is always a way to get through it, right? Yes, there must be a way to get through it, if only May would arrive -

(When May arrives, there will be the sounds of selling plums on the streets and in the alleys; there will also be many different moods on the streets and in the alleys. Big, black patrol cars, as stubborn as shadows, often appear on the road.)

The wind gradually picks up, May is a season that is more suitable for leisure. People (a portion of them) leave the tension and chaos of the metropolis, and like poets, go to the countryside with leisurely hearts, changing into light, thin outing clothes, bringing cars, canes, lovely wives, binoculars, cameras...

Thus, to the metropolis, to the streets and alleys lying within it: "May is not suitable for the metropolis; may this be a pleasant short trip, and may this May be peaceful!"

If April is prose, then May will definitely be romance.

Mountain Road 219

— Hua Jia

Our hike this time is adventurous. Among the three companions, two have never walked this rugged mountain road before. In my memory, this is also an unfamiliar road, but I had walked it two years ago. We probably won't encounter any villages within twenty miles, but tonight we have to rush to a certain village about thirty miles from here.

On both sides are very high and steep cliffs, bare and without any trees or larger plants. I believe that even woodcutters wouldn't come to these places. However, in this mountainous area, such small paths are already considered the only transportation routes. We originally didn't want to come to this place. However, for the sake of that small school's employment contract and the alluring "profession," we three young people forgot about the hardship, because we felt the threat of unemployment and the terror of life. So we had no choice but to walk this unfamiliar and rugged mountain road to honor a friend's invitation and the warmth of a profession.

This area was originally not very accessible, and there are no waterways, so whenever something happens, you have to run. As usual, from the province, take the wheel-tow ferry unique to these two Guangxi provinces to where the water runs out, then go ashore. Once ashore, there are some highway buses waiting for passengers. After taking the bus to the county seat, running is already very close, only about seven or eight miles. However, recently, because of several days of heavy rain, the unstable highway has become muddy and impassable for cars, so everyone has to run. The local people are used to running, but it's no joke for us outsiders to come here and run this long thirty-odd miles.

It's okay to run at the beginning, there are villages, paddy fields, trees, and thatched huts. But when it comes to the end, there's only a mountain road flanked by cliffs on both sides. Moreover, according to the villagers, this mountain road will extend to twenty miles, and it's very close when you see fields of tobacco plants. We have to finish this mountain road, which is longer than thirty miles, this afternoon.

In the silent and terrifying mountain road, we can only rely on each other's courage and the burning heart fire of young people to light the way, and everyone is fearless and marching forward, like a team of soldiers attacking their enemies.

Sometimes we would complain, shouldn't have come to this mountainous area to find terror and trouble. However, a moment of courage encouraged us. We are still young, this little bit of hardship is not much, because we are going to "find food!" So we walked our unfamiliar mountain road with even bigger strides.

A burst of tobacco smell rushed into our nostrils. We felt an extraordinary pleasure. The mountain road has ended again, the green tobacco fields are rippling in front of us, and we are more happily accelerating this terrible journey to find the warmth of a profession.

Along the Longyou River 220

— Yuan Zhi

The night is like a thin silk veil, already enveloping the winding Longyou River.

Longyou River, what an elegant and uniquely stylish name. Just like its name, this river is elegant, with scattered shrubs and a green expanse of creeping grass and colorful wildflowers lining its banks. The river flows from the far west, winding and turning, like a long giant dragon. Any boats passing through this river, even if it's just a small bamboo leaf boat, cannot sail any faster. If you're impatient, it's no use. You have to slowly steer the oars left and right, crossing the surface of the river, before you can dispose of it according to your own intentions.

The water in the river is very clear, because the river's mouth connects to the lake, such a flowing stream, naturally not afraid of being polluted or the boat's oars stirring up the yellow mud at the bottom of the river, making the water turbid.

Relying on this river, thousands of acres of paddy fields and mulberry fields have bumper harvests every year, which is also where hundreds of households survive. They are all the children of the Longyou River, they are grateful and cherish it.

Besides the hundreds of households, the Longyou River also has an adopted son - the only fishing family that survives by it.

This fishing family is downstream of the Longyou River. A low, simple thatched shed is where they live and rest. An old fisherman, an old woman who is almost the same, and a young son live in the house.

The three people have lived here for a long time. The old couple remember very clearly, they rowed a small boat out of their hometown and lived by fishing here, gradually being able to build this shed with a few loads of mud and a few loads of thatch; later, how they bought a big dragnet and raised such a son. The old couple are even clearer that they are where they are now entirely because of the Longyou River's gift. The river is their hometown, the river is their factory.

In the twilight, it was no longer possible to distinguish everything clearly. The old fisherman standing next to the winch of the big dragnet raised his voice and shouted:

"Little Gouzi's mother, why haven't you lit the mast light yet?"

Little Gouzi's mother was cooking dinner by the stove. The stove without a chimney sent all the smoke around Little Gouzi's mother, making it impossible for her old eyes to open properly. Hearing the old man's shout outside, just as she was about to stand up, the old fisherman shouted again:

"Are you deaf? Such an irresponsible old woman... Hurry up, there's a big black carp in the net!"

While shouting, he worked the "handle" on the winch of the big dragnet even harder. He felt the net getting heavier and heavier; he thought, there must be a big black carp in the net; it probably swam upstream from the lake. This fish must weigh twenty or thirty pounds, haha, it would sell for several big silver dollars. Thinking about it, he couldn't help but become happier, a layer of smile spreading across his face.

The old woman brought the mast light. A tiny spark of light couldn't shine more than ten feet away. She hung it on a bamboo hook in front of the thatched shed, then walked close to the winch to help the old fisherman wind it. The two of them used all their remaining strength, their hearts full of extreme joy.

It just so happened that the son who had gone to the street to buy wine also came back, so he also came to help, winding and winding, hanging a large net high above the river. The son hurriedly went to fish with the "fish net," but no matter how hard he tried, he couldn't catch anything, so he couldn't help but become suspicious. When the old fisherman went to check with the mast light, a swollen child's corpse was lying stiffly in the net, and he couldn't help but shout "Ah -- yo".

Under the Wisteria Trellis 221

— Chen Li'ang

This afternoon, I walked out of the house with a cigarette, so relaxed, without a single worry lingering in my mood. Before lunch, I had planned to do quite a few things. The letter from home had been put aside for five days and should be replied to. I couldn't find a single pair of intact socks in my suitcase, so I should buy some. The inkstone had a thick layer of ink, so I should wash it... But, when I took the first puff of my cigarette, I thought those things could wait. Sometimes I myself would wonder, "Why am I so lazy?" For many days, I had been living with this laziness.

My nature is to love leisure, but my environment has no leisure. I stubbornly want to extract leisure from busyness, abandoning what I should be doing and intentionally idling, without feeling uneasy or caring about other people's opinions. I believe that only in leisure can I truly appreciate the true interest of life. Although this is not true leisure, I am still very satisfied. How many people in this worldly world are not hurrying and worrying about their own lives? How many people can obtain a truly leisurely life?

This is indeed a habit I have developed. I will get rid of all trivial matters, but I also hurry for the sake of life. Sometimes sweat beads seep from my forehead, blisters appear on the soles of my feet, my arms move until they are sore, and my mind is entangled and dizzy by the shapes and colors of the outside world. However, my state of mind is often leisurely. In the public car, I will smoke and read the newspaper's supplement, so much so that sometimes I even forget the date. My friends say I am too muddleheaded, and I do not deny it. Perhaps in this era, in this world, only the muddleheaded can feel some joy.

So I sat with a cigarette under the wisteria trellis in the courtyard. The rain had stimulated the flowers to bloom, and the rain had also knocked the flowers off. Petals scattered on the courtyard ground made of soil, like a piece of bluish-gray cloth woven with purple floral dots, possessing a quiet and beautiful feeling. Therefore, the attraction of this beauty also crushed my soul, shattered it, and scattered it with the petals on the wet and slippery brick ground.

The courtyard is dilapidated everywhere, even the wisteria trellis is very decayed and on the verge of collapsing. The columns near the ground are wearing green moss leggings. The leaves and flowers are sparser year by year. I don't know if it's because it's old and withered, or if it's adapting to the environment of the decaying trellis. However, I also love this unhealthy, morbid appearance. I am still fortunate that the family of my courtyard owner has declined, otherwise, this old-fashioned tile house, the mossy wooden frame, the graceful wisteria, the green jade-like leaves, and the purple, cold, and beautiful flower petals would have long been replaced by cement, iron bones, red lacquer, stone blocks, and the ugly materials of modern civilization.

People's loves and hates are different. Many people may frown and say that my residence is filled with decadence and death, they love the ogre-like Western buildings, the pruned holly, the goldfish in the white stone pond, the iron railings, and the large flowers with stimulating colors. But these things, in our eyes, are ugly and vulgar. I am not used to contacting that rich and noble atmosphere, and I can't bear to see those people who are competing in the arena of fame and fortune without knowing when to rest. Perhaps they are also accusing me of being eccentric and narrow-minded at the same time!

However, I still feel at ease. Every day, I will still steal some leisure to sit under the wisteria trellis, smoking, and reading a little of my favorite books. At this time, I will forget what I should be doing, and what I should be recalling about the past. Under the wisteria trellis, you can't find any hurried emotions, any thoughts of fame and fortune, or any rich and noble atmosphere.

Supplement to the Shanghai Shen Bao Local Edition Movie Special Issue

The Making of the Newsreel of the Hauptmann Kidnapping Trial (Part Two) 225

— Xin Ni

From the above conversation with Clifford, we can see that filming sound movies in the courtroom was not illegal, but was done with the express permission of the judge. However, the cameraman also had his tricks, which we can describe.

According to the American film industry's authoritative journal, "Film Daily," Judge Trenchard had instructed beforehand that the filming of newsreels in the courtroom was limited to times when the defendant was not being interrogated in the dock. That is, only the prisoner's idle movements and conversations could be filmed, not his state while being tried in the dock.

However, the company's cameramen deliberately violated this order. To be cautious and prevent news reporters from secretly filming, the court specifically ordered the bailiffs to turn off all the special lights installed for photography inside the courtroom when the prisoner entered the dock, and to lower the curtains halfway, dimming the courtroom and preventing secret filming. However, modern photography techniques deceived the judge, because the cameraman used extremely fast lenses and specially made extremely fast film to capture all the courtroom scenes while the prisoner was on trial.

Of course, when filming such a movie, there could be no sound of the camera's mechanism moving. This also required a special silent device to be installed on the camera beforehand. Furthermore, no one could stand next to the camera, but rather be hidden dozens of feet away, cutting the wires and using the intermittent current to control the camera's movements. Of course, these skills cannot be successfully executed by someone who is not experienced in this field.

However, we must also raise the second question: should such films of criminals be made, and do they have intrinsic value? On this point, New York District Attorney Dodge and criminologist Dodge made the following statement:

"Generally speaking, I am against and advocate banning all films, whether short newsreels or feature dramas, that depict the actions of criminals and suspected criminals. I believe that such films will have a bad influence after coming into contact with children. Even adults, if their minds and thoughts are not mature, may be led astray by the misunderstanding of heroism and glory inherent in the acts of crime and violations of criminal law seen in criminal films.

"As for the film of the Hauptmann trial, I don't think it's as bad. The way the prisoner cowered and felt ashamed under District Attorney Wilentz's burning gaze and sharp tongue is enough to show that a person who commits a crime can never escape the law. Not only is breaking the law not a broad road, but even after being arrested, one cannot simply die to end it all.

"That kind of mental suffering shows that anyone with awareness can know that after committing a crime, a person's bravery and composure to die are useless, and they have no choice but to tremble with fear, wanting to die but unable to. But to most people, it's just giving a German carpenter unparalleled publicity."

"In any case, I believe that such films should not be shown publicly until the criminal has been convicted."

The above is the opinion of a New York prosecutor, and also the majority opinion of American prosecutors. Now we will listen to the opinion of a famous lawyer and criminal defense attorney, Samuel Leibowitz.

Leibowitz's opinion is: "Not only have I not seen that newsreel, but I don't want to see it either. I think that kind of film should not be watched by anyone. I am extremely opposed to such sensational publicity about a criminal or a crime. I believe this is a common problem with American news policy. But since we have allowed many news reporters and novelists to sit in the courtroom and use their subjective pens to describe the prisoner's trembling in the witness stand, why should we make things difficult for the news photographers and not allow them to go a step further and give the prisoner an even more vivid portrait with sound and color? Of course, the film is clear and undeniable, but the news reporters' writing is somewhat unreliable. One says the prisoner was trembling with shame, while another says the prisoner was calm and unafraid of death. Who knows who is right?

"If our trial system adopted the dignified attitude of England, instead of the current circus-like situation with three classes of spectators, the filming of newsreels would certainly not be a problem.

In short, I don't want to see this film. It's not because I don't need to see the courtroom situation again, but because I fundamentally disapprove of everyone watching it, because spending money to watch it is encouraging the production of such films, and indirectly encouraging treating the courtroom as a joke and the trial as a circus.

"As for the cameraman violating the court order and secretly filming, it is especially despicable and hateful and should be severely punished." (End)

Film Review

Review of "Fallen Blossoms" 226

— Zhao Ren

——Xin Guang Films

Since "The Big Wind," director Wu Cun has appeared on the Chinese film scene with a new attitude. People have high expectations for him, believing that he will give us a lot of fresh artistic food.

Yes, this young director has the passion and courage to face reality squarely. He has a resentful mood and expresses his denial of the current society. He has a righteous passion and shows his jealousy towards ugliness. However, he is also an overly clever artist. He understands the wisdom of dealing with the world too well, so he is unwilling to make a frontal attack on the evils of the world, but only tries to touch the ugliness from the side with delicate brushstrokes, trying to insert some pungent irony into people's laughter. However, due to the rawness of his expression techniques, he cannot grasp the object he wants to express. He does not not criticize reality, but does not know how to criticize it. Even if it is ironic exposure, he cannot sharply touch the inner secrets of noble people. Therefore, his irony is only superficial and symbolic, like the big wind blowing off the gentleman's top hat or the lady's underwear in "The Big Wind". Similarly, in the contrast between positive and negative sides, he does not have the confidence to sympathize with the people he wants to sympathize with.

More importantly, his works show a very strong intellectual flavor. His vision is very broad, and his desire for self-satisfaction is also very strong. He wants to express everything he can feel in one work. He is unwilling and unable to filter his emotions and focus on a certain main purpose. Therefore, his passionate and uninhibited outpouring seems disorganized and chaotic in his works, as if he has not organized his materials.

However, his passionate expression only surges in "The Big Wind." In "Fallen Blossoms," he seems to have suffered some major blow, expressing his pessimism in a sad atmosphere. Now let's take a closer look at "Fallen Blossoms."

"Fallen Blossoms," like "The Big Wind," expresses a good intention. It depicts the arduous battles of the Volunteer Army, without internal support and with exhausted supplies. The Volunteer Army was sacrificed and defeated under the pressure of a strong enemy. On the one hand, the author says in the mouth of the soldier Zhao Dan that even hand-to-hand combat must be resisted to the end. On the other hand, he expresses his grief for national affairs with the intellectual's sigh, "Flowing water, fallen flowers, spring is gone." Here, using fallen flowers to set off the defeat of the national war is certainly inappropriate. In the midst of the cruel war, the poet's sighs of fallen flowers and flowing water and the melancholy of a woman in her boudoir can never match the tragedy of the national war. …This sadness of fallen flowers continues until Ah Xuan's death. There are also fallen flowers in the workers' basement and in the hospital. …The sadness continues throughout. However, later he also felt that this was not very good, so in another season of fallen flowers, the war clouds in North China are urgent. The soldiers go to the front line again, coming to a positive ending that is the opposite of sadness. However, this positivity disappears in the sad atmosphere, that is to say, sadness is the main thing the author describes, and the positive ending is just to show that he has no choice but to do so.

In some minor details, we may be able to see some degree of progress in the author, such as in "The Big Wind," where the wind is used symbolically to satirize the hypocrisy of gentlemen and ladies, while in "Fallen Blossoms," he uses the printing workers to tear up the gorgeous evening gowns. However, in terms of expression techniques, the author is still unable to go beyond the scope of intellectuals. He is not familiar with high society, just as he is not familiar with lower-class life. He relies entirely on his own imagination, plus the inherent romanticism, so he cannot give people any sense of reality. Perhaps we admit that he progressed more smoothly in "Remarriage," because it only wrote about familiar things that intellectuals have experienced. He cannot organize the plot more rigorously, and like "The Big Wind," the front and back are not connected, such as suddenly writing about a fashion company from the basement, which the audience does not understand at all. In addition, the several flashbacks and backstories are unfamiliar to the general audience. Xu Lai's scars, besides the business-minded display, we don't know the source of the scars. …There is no need to say more.

In short, in "Fallen Blossoms," because the author has not clearly defined the personalities of the characters in the play, except that Zhao Dan knows how to act and is very energetic, there is not much achievement in terms of acting skills.

Chinese Movie Star Panorama Sells Well 227

The "Chinese Movie Star Panorama" published by Yisheng Publishing House on the 6th floor of 133 Yuanmingyuan Road is rich, beautiful, and unprecedented. Since its publication, purchases have come from far and near. The local newspapers have unanimously praised it as the most noble and valuable publication in the modern film publishing industry. The general social circles also use this book as a topic of conversation. The remaining copies of the first edition are few, so buyers must be quick to avoid missing out.

The new movie "Fallen Blossoms" starring Xu Lai, etc., directed by Wu Cun, is showing at Xin Guang Films.

Movie Novel

The Devil is a Woman (Part One) 228

— Wen Ying

Produced by Paramount Pictures, starring Marlene Dietrich

Concha is a famous Spanish dancer. She has unparalleled beauty. Her clear autumn eyes have caused many men to lose their souls. Her clear, oriole-like voice still lingers in their ears after their pasts have become like smoke. But she is ultimately a fleeting cloud in their eyes, elusive, because Concha is beautiful but heartless, using love as a game and beauty as a hook to attract men and women.

I don't know how many hundreds or thousands of people have passed through her life. She doesn't remember their names clearly. They all admired her and fell at her slender feet, but when she fell out of favor, she didn't bother to kick them. She showed them one by one that she was tired of them. She shrugged her fragrant shoulders, revealing a "I am tired and want to sleep, you can leave" expression. The lover of last night has now awakened from a dream, realizing that the good times cannot be kept, and retreats.

But one of them was unwilling to be slighted, unwilling to be summoned and dismissed like the others. He was Don Pasquale. He was tall and strong, and his temperament was violent, but he had a deep love for Concha and was willing to die for love. His family was noble and he held an important position in the military. Concha felt that his position and wealth could be used, so she often pretended to be amorous, and Pasquale was infatuated and obeyed her every command. In this way, Concha and her greedy mother took from him without asking, and Pasquale obeyed their every command in order to win the beauty's heart.

Although Pasquale's family was wealthy, how could it withstand Concha's insatiable demands? After a period of time, Pasquale had reached the point where his money was running out, and he was helpless. Not only was his wealth exhausted and his family ruined, but he also lost his reputation and could no longer serve in the military. His military position had to be resigned because of this. After this disillusionment, his love turned into hatred. He vowed to use the rest of his life to warn other young people to stay away from the snake-hearted dancer.

It was the Carnival in Andalusia, and a guest from afar had arrived. He was a handsome young man with a beautiful face. His name was Antonio Galván. He should not have set foot on Spanish soil, because he was wanted by the government for promoting republicanism and inciting revolution, and had fled the country. This time, because he missed his mother so much, he disguised himself and risked his life to return home to see her. He was walking down the street with flags waving and flowers blooming, when suddenly he saw an unparalleled beauty. He couldn't help but stare at her in fascination, and his breathing stopped.

That's right, the woman he saw was none other than the red dancer of Spain, Concha. She was sitting in a magnificent carriage and sped past Antonio. In a state of confusion, Antonio unknowingly followed closely behind her carriage, all the way to her house.

Strangely, Concha was not angry when she saw the handsome young man, but was rather happy, because it was her favorite thing to have such a handsome young man fall in love with her at first sight. He didn't know that this was Concha's old trick of hooking new romances. He begged her to agree to meet him again tomorrow afternoon. She readily agreed.

The next day, Antonio was about to keep his appointment, but he unexpectedly ran into Pasquale. Because Pasquale was also an old friend of his, Antonio told Pasquale all about his adventure during their conversation. (To be continued)
